COMMITTEE REPORTS  
 
CR 24-42  Recommending the following:  
1. ADOPTION of Resolution 24-52 to authorize the acquisition of a one-bedroom, 
one-bathroom unit at the Kahana Manor condominium project, consisting of 631 
square feet, located at 4310 Lower Honoapiilani Road, Apt. No. 617, Lah aina, 
Maui, Hawaii, for $530,000, exclusive of closing costs and expenses;  
2. ADOPTION of Resolution 24-53 to authorize the acquisition of a one-bedroom, 
one-bathroom unit at the Parkview Square condominium project, consisting of 
696 square feet, located at 1129 Lower Main Street, Apt. No. 303, Wailuku, Maui, 
Hawaii, for $440,000, exclusive of closing costs and expenses; and  
3. ADOPTION of Resolution 24-54 to authorize the acquisition of a two-bedroom, 
one-bathroom unit at the Keonekai Villages condominium project, consisting of 
625 square feet, located at 160 Keonekai Road, Unit 13-101, Kihei, Maui, Hawaii, 
for $625,000, exclusive of closing costs and expenses.  
 
 
CR 24-43 Recommending the following:  
1. FIRST READING of Bill 48, CD1 (2024) to amend the Fiscal Year 2024 Budget, 
by: 1) amending Section 2, Estimated Revenues, by increasing Other 
Intergovernmental by $1,502,403; 
2) amending Section 4.H.1.a., Department of Water Supply, Countywide, Water 
Supply, by adding a new appropriation for State Rev olving Loan Fund, entitled 
“Lead and Copper Rule Revision Compliance,” in the amount of $1,502,403; 3) 
adjusting the totals accordingly; and 4) amending Appendix C - Capital 
Improvement Projects, Department of Water Supply, Countywide, by adding a 
new project and project description, entitled “Lead and Copper Rule Revision 
Compliance,” in the amount of $1,502,403; and  
2. FIRST READING of Bill 49 (2024) to authorize the Mayor to enter into an 
intergovernmental agreement with the State of Hawaii for a loan f rom the 
Drinking Water State Revolving Fund in the amount of $1,502,403 for Lead and 
Copper Rule Revision Compliance.
